Q1. What is the new phone sharing system implemented by the Social Security Administration (SSA)?
A. Calls to local field offices are rerouted to available staff at other field offices, regardless of geographic location, to help manage high call volumes.
B. Calls to local field offices are rerouted to staff who don't have jurisdiction over the caller's case.
C. Calls to local field offices are rerouted to staff who have jurisdiction over the caller's case.
D. Calls to local field offices are not rerouted to any other field offices.
Correct Answer: A

Q2. According to Angela Digeronimo, what does the new phone sharing system create for people calling into their local office?
A. A "hit or miss" situation for people calling in to their local office.
B. A situation where it is taking more time to help people get and keep Social Security disability benefits.
C. A situation where workers in other field offices can see what's going on with someone's case but can't "actually take care of the issue."
D. A situation where all SSA field offices are equipped to handle inquiries and resolve issues for callers, irrespective of where a caller lives or where their case originated.
Correct Answer: A

A. It is taking her group "more time to help people" get and keep Social Security disability benefits.
B. It is creating a situation where it is taking more time to help people get and keep Social Security disability benefits.
C. It is creating a situation where workers in other field offices can see what's going on with someone's case but can't "actually take care of the issue."
D. It is creating a situation where all SSA field offices are equipped to handle inquiries and resolve issues for callers, irrespective of where a caller lives or where their case originated.

Correct Answer: A. The American Manufacturing Program

Q3. What is the specific goal of the American Manufacturing Program announced by Apple?
A. To ensure that iPhones sold in the United States are made in America
B. To shift iPhone production to India to avoid tariffs
C. To increase investment in the United States
D. To produce components for Apple products sold all over the world
Correct Answer: A. To ensure that iPhones sold in the United States are made in America
